<div class="para">商业的繁荣带动了<a target=_blank href="/view/429288.htm">手工业</a>等行业的发展<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />形成了竹器街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />面街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />棉花街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />弹花街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />打石街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />打锁街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />皮糖街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />猪糠街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />风炉街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />豆腐巷<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />蒜头街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />果栏街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />线香街等产品专卖街和作坊<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />工厂等<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>

<div class="para">传说<a target=_blank href="/subview/722684/11045519.htm">石龙</a>作为一个开墟开始于<a target=_blank href="/subview/3371/13497972.htm">明朝</a><a target=_blank />距城北三十里<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />有镇曰石龙<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" <div class="para">明末清初著名学家曾在<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=108932030168486474428289659" /><a target=_blank href="/view/420464.htm">广东新语</a><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=881584074518235945079112911" />中写道<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=820013475104505573524673609" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />石龙亦邑之一会<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />其地千树荔<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />千亩潮蔗<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />桔柚蕉柑次之……<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" />盛赞石龙物产之丰富<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para"><a target=_blank href="/view/660261.htm">道光</a>二十年<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=627490465706796950862818540" />1840<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=989590432809781566698481752" />鸦片战争后<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />石龙的经济更加繁荣<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />这与和<a target=_blank href="/view/2607.htm">香港</a>以及其他资本主义国家贸易来往有关<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />与资本主义国家的贸易交往日益密切<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />使石龙人的语言也发生了改变<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />并逐步开始设厂生产<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" /><a target=_blank href="/subview/867715/14821075.htm">洋货</a><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">从乾隆年间起到日军占领石龙这二百年间<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />石龙是<a target=_blank href="/view/26226.htm">东莞</a>经济最繁荣的城镇<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div><h3 class="headline-2"><a name="4_2" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="sub7967032_4_2" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="商贾如云_民国初年" class="anchor-2"></a><span class="headline-content">民国初年</span></h3><div class="para"><a target=_blank href="/view/691086.htm">广九铁路</a>于1911年10月通车<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" /><a target=_blank href="/subview/77262/5037777.htm">民国</a>元年<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=627490465706796950862818540" />1912<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=989590432809781566698481752" />年开始办理旅客和货运业务<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />这一下子改变了以东江流域客货运输为主的局面<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />铁路与轮船的交替使用<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />使只适应水路运输的行业不得不倒闭<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />同时洋货大量流入<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />特别是便宜且漂亮的洋布<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />直接冲击了石龙的棉纺织业<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />仅仅民国初的几年<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />石龙商店倒闭将近30%<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">石龙地处东江流域咽喉<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />交通要塞<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />故是东江流域一个军事要塞<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /><a target=_blank href="/view/104372.htm">1916年</a>至<a target=_blank href="/view/673033.htm">1929年</a>这十多年间的战乱<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />使石龙商业以及整个经济遭到沉重打击<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div><h3 class="headline-2"><a name="4_3" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="sub7967032_4_3" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="商贾如云_改革开放" class="anchor-2"></a><span class="headline-content">改革开放</span></h3><div class="para">商风鼎盛传统的石龙镇<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />得<a target=_blank href="/view/48598.htm">改革开放</a>春风之先<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />大力发展商品经济和高科技<div class="text_pic layoutright" data-layout="right" style="width:220px;padding-left: 20px"><a href="/picview/327591/7967032/0/d048addebcb2a31bccbf1ad0.html?fr=lemma" class="lemmapic-mask use-picture-dialog" target="_blank" style="width:220px;height:176px;left: 20px"

<div class="para">铁矾土虽有<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />但很<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />嫩<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />1959年曾开掘<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />但终无采用<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">冬季<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />镇区水井的水面有时有油光<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />据说地底有石油<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />但<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />嫩<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />无开采价值<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div><div class="anchor-list"><a name="16" class="anchor-1"></a><a name="sub7967032_16" class="anchor-1"></a><a name="非物质文化遗产" class="anchor-1"></a></div><h2 class="headline-1"><span class="headline-1-index">16</span><span class="headline-content">非物质文化遗产</span><span class="text_edit editable-title" style="margin-left: 10px;" data-edit-id="4377685:%E7%9F%B3%E9%BE%99%E9%95%87:16"><a href="#" class="nslog:1019" title="编辑本段">编辑</a></span></h2><div class="para">新昌鼓</div>
